SELECT CASE WHEN T_ALL = T_CNT1 THEN '01' -- 전부 승인이면 승인 WHEN T_ALL = T_CNT2 THEN '02' -- 전부 불승인이면 불승인 WHEN T_CNT3 > 0 THEN '03' -- 보류 1개이상시 보류 WHEN T_CNT4 > 0 THEN '90' -- 반려 1개이상시 반려 WHEN MINWON_DOC_CD <> '6003' AND T_CNT5 > 0 THEN '02' -- 공동주택아니고 30임미만 1개이상시 불승인 WHEN MINWON_DOC_CD <> '6003' AND T_CNT6 > 0 THEN '02' -- 공동주택아니고 최저임금 1개이상시 불승인 WHEN MINWON_DOC_CD <> '6003' AND T_CNT1 > 0 AND T_CNT5 = 0 AND T_CNT6 = 0 THEN '01' -- 공동주택아니고 지원원별 승인 1개이상이고 최저임금, 30민미만이 없으면 승인(일부승인) WHEN MINWON_DOC_CD = '6003' AND T_CNT1 > 0 THEN '01' -- 공동주택이고 지원원별 승인 1개이상이면 승인(일부승인) ELSE '00' -- 해당하는 조건 없음 END AS RESULT FROM (SELECT COUNT(C.JEOPSU_NO) AS T_ALL -- 전체 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_SIMSA_RESULT_CD IN ('01','04') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT1 -- 승인 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_SIMSA_RESULT_CD IN ('02','05') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT2 -- 불승인 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_SIMSA_RESULT_CD IN ('03','06') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT3 -- 보류 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_SIMSA_RESULT_CD = '90' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT4 -- 반려 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.MN30_MIMAN_FG IN ('02','05') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT5 -- 30인미만임금 불승인건 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.CHOEJEO_IMGEUM_FG IN ('02','05') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT6 -- 최저임금 불승인건 , MAX(B.MINWON_DOC_CD) AS MINWON_DOC_CD -- 민원서식 , MIN(A.SIMSA_JINHAENG_STATUS_CD) AS SIMSA_JINHAENG_STATUS_CD -- 심사진행상태 FROM US_IOWN.IJB050MT A JOIN US_IOWN.IAA100MT C ON C.ILJARI_NO = A.ILJARI_NO LEFT OUTER JOIN US_IOWN.IQA500MT B ON B.JEOPSU_NO = C.JEOPSU_NO WHERE A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO = :B1 -- 대표일자리번호 AND A.JIWON_YEAR = :B2 AND A.JEONGGI_CNT = :B3 AND A.SIMSA_CNT = (SELECT MAX(Z.SIMSA_CNT) FROM US_IOWN.IJB050MT Z WHERE Z.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO = A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO AND Z.JIWON_YEAR = A.JIWON_YEAR AND Z.JEONGGI_CNT = A.JEONGGI_CNT ) )

INSERT INTO IKA050MT_IFS ( EAI_JEONSONG_SER , DAESANG_DATE , TOTAL_COUNT , DAY_COUNT , COUNT_RATE , INSERT_DATE , EAI_DML_YUHYEONG , EAI_SAENGSEONG_ILSI , EAI_JEONSONG_YN ) SELECT SQ_EIS_DAILY_JOB_SER.NEXTVAL AS EAI_JEONSONG_SER , TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'YYYYMMDD'), 'YYYYMMDD') AS DAESANG_DATE , Y.NJ_CNT AS TOTAL_COUNT , Y.DI_CNT AS DAY_COUNT , DECODE(Y.BEF_CNT, 0, 0, NVL(ROUND(((Y.DI_CNT - Y.BEF_CNT)/Y.BEF_CNT)*100, 2), 0)) AS JG_CNT_PCT , SYSDATE AS INSERT_DATE , DECODE(NVL(Y.TODAY_YN, 'I'), 'Y', 'U', 'I') AS EAI_DML_YUHYEONG , SYSDATE AS EAI_SAENGSEONG_ILSI , 'N' AS EAI_JEONSONG_YN FROM (SELECT ZZ.DT , NVL(MAX(NJ_CNT),0) NJ_CNT , NVL(MAX(DI_CNT),0) DI_CNT , NVL(MAX(BEF_CNT),0) BEF_CNT , (SELECT 'Y' FROM IKA050MT_IFS C WHERE C.DAESANG_DATE = TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'YYYYMMDD'), 'YYYYMMDD') AND ROWNUM = 1) AS TODAY_YN FROM ( SELECT '1' , TO_CHAR(SYSDATE,'YYYYMMDD') AS DT , COUNT(DISTINCT AA.ILJARI_NO ||AA.GEUNROJA_NO) AS NJ_CNT , 0 AS DI_CNT , 0 AS BEF_CNT FROM (SELECT D.ILJARI_NO, E.GEUNROJA_NO FROM (SELECT ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO, SUM(JIGEUP_PRC) AS JIGEUP_PRC, MIN(FBS_JIGEUP_DT) AS FBS_JIGEUP_DT FROM IBC250MT WHERE FBS_JIGEUP_UIROE_FG = '2' AND FBS_JIGEUP_RESULT_CD = '0000' GROUP BY ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO ) C , IBB010MT D , IBB020MT E WHERE D.JIGEUP_JEOPSU_NO = C.JEOPSU_NO AND E.JEOPSU_NO = D.JEOPSU_NO AND E.ILJARI_NO = D.ILJARI_NO AND E.JIWON_YEAR = D.JIWON_YEAR AND E.JIWON_MM = D.JIWON_MM AND E.JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC > 0 AND C.FBS_JIGEUP_DT <= TO_CHAR(SYSDATE,'YYYYMMDD') UNION SELECT D.ILJARI_NO, E.GEUNROJA_NO FROM (SELECT ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO, SUM(JIGEUP_PRC) AS JIGEUP_PRC, MIN(FBS_JIGEUP_DT) AS FBS_JIGEUP_DT FROM IBC250MT WHERE FBS_JIGEUP_UIROE_FG = '2' AND FBS_JIGEUP_RESULT_CD = '0000' GROUP BY ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO ) C , IBB110MT D , IBB120MT E WHERE D.ILJARI_NO = C.ILJARI_NO AND C.JEOPSU_NO = E.JIGEUP_JEOPSU_NO AND D.ILJARI_NO = E.ILJARI_NO AND D.JIWON_YEAR = E.JIWON_YEAR AND
